      <p style="text-align: center;"><img src="/images/smicollage.gif" alt="banner" width="480" height="299" /></p> 
      <div class="spotlight" style="padding-bottom: 0px; background: white;"> 
       <h3>Inspire the Future, <br />Become a Science or Mathematics Teacher</h3> 
      </div>
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
      <p></p> 
      <div class="column23"> 
       <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="column2" group="Everyone" button="657" -->
       <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="315"/ -->
       <h4><span style="color: #000000;">Why is </span><strong><span style="color: #990000;">NOW</span></strong><span style="color: #000000;"> the time to prepare for a career in teaching science and mathematics?</span></h4> 
       <p>There is currently a critical shortfall of qualified science and mathematics teachers in California classrooms. Because of this shortage, prospective science and mathematics teachers are extremely competitive in securing positions soon after graduation.</p> 
       <p>They are able to:</p> 
       <ul class="star"> 
        <li>find internship jobs immediately upon graduation at salaries comparable to entry-level credentialed teachers; these intern opportunities often lead to permanent teaching positions</li> 
        <li>find job openings in the school district of their desire</li> 
        <li>become emerging leaders in the school districts and communities</li> 
        <li>benefit from the financial incentives, including loan-forgiveness programs, offered through the government<a href="https://www.facebook.com/ScienceMathInitiativeAtUcr"><img src="/images/facebook.jpg" alt="smi facebook" width="270" height="187" /></a></li> 
       </ul> 
       <p><a href="http://calteach.universityofcalifornia.edu/"><strong>UCR-SMI is part of the UC-system wide California Teach - Science and mathematics Initiative</strong></a></p> 
       <p><strong><strong><img src="/images/calteach-logo.gif" alt="uc-smi logo" width="240" height="68" /></strong></strong></p> 
       <p><strong>Read about UC-systemwide SMI/<a href="http://www.universityofcalifornia.edu/news/article/26983">&quot;CalTeach &quot;brings STEM students into K-12 classrooms</a>.</strong></p> 
       <p>&nbsp;</p>
       <!-- /com.omniupdate.div --> 
      </div> 
      <div class="column3R on_the_side"> 
       <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="column3R" group="Everyone" button="657" -->
       <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="145"/ -->

        <div class="yom-mod yom-featuredroll" id="mediafeaturedrolllpcatemp">
         <div class="bd">
          <ul>
           <li class="newpage yom-featuredroll-content yom-featuredroll-MediaModelStory">
            <div class="yom-mod" id="mediafeaturedrolllpcatemp">
             <div class="hd">
              <div class="yom-featuredroll-hd">
               <div class="headline">
                <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/baker-erin-mckenna-on-success--make-things-happen-for-yourself-185948785.html" mapleultparams="pkg=a6cd4fd0-8816-3aa9-adfd-080042499b65;ver=3f368002-10dd-11e3-ade1-75ae9d07a8c3;pos=1">Baker Erin McKenna on Success: Make Things Happen For Yourself</a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/secrets-to-your-success-ycn-1675353/" mapleultparams="pos=1">Secrets To Your Success</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/secrets-to-your-success/">Secrets to Your Success</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2013-08-29T18:59:47Z">Thu, Aug 29, 2013 2:59 PM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/secrets-to-your-success/baker-erin-mckenna-on-success--make-things-happen-for-yourself-185948785.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>
             </div>
             <div class="bd">
              <iframe src="http://shine.yahoo.com/video/playlist/secrets-to-your-success/erin-mckenna-founder-babycakes-nyc-230000632.html?format=embed&amp;show_carousel=true&amp;player_autoplay=false" data-yom-embed-source="{media_id_1:1da6afdc-b620-3548-b46e-86686fbce096}" frameborder="0" height="495" width="634"></iframe>
              <p>When Erin McKenna decided to opened a specialty bakery in 2005, she had very little baking experience and had never run a business.&nbsp; But she taught herself to bake vegan, gluten-free, and soy-free goods, one recipe at a time. The business lessons came on the fly. Once year after she opened the doors of <a>Babycakes NYC</a>, her cupcakes were named the best in New York.</p>
              <p>&quot;It wasn't just best gluten-free or vegan cupcake,&quot; said McKenna. &quot;It was just best across the board.&nbsp; But it was this — such huge praise.&nbsp; So it was very much overwhelming and a beautiful moment for me.&quot;</p>
              <p><a href="http://yhoo.it/1a2zI8b">More on Shine: Top 8 Food Allergies (and How to Eat Around Them)</a></p>Before working in the food industry, McKenna had a brief stint with a fashion magazine.&nbsp; Shortly after leaving her magazine job, she came up with the idea of a bakery for people with food allergies. McKenna's interest in creating and selling vegan, gluten-free, soy-free, and wheat-free baked goods stems from her personal experience with food allergies. As a child, s...
              <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/baker-erin-mckenna-on-success--make-things-happen-for-yourself-185948785.html" class="read-more" mapleultparams="pkg=a6cd4fd0-8816-3aa9-adfd-080042499b65;ver=3f368002-10dd-11e3-ade1-75ae9d07a8c3;pos=1">Read More&nbsp;&raquo;</a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <hr /></li>
           <li class="newpage yom-featuredroll-content yom-featuredroll-MediaModelStory">
            <div class="yom-mod" id="mediafeaturedrolllpcatemp">
             <div class="hd">
              <div class="yom-featuredroll-hd">
               <div class="headline">
                <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/keeping-peace-38-co-worker-want-same-promotion-175300121.html" mapleultparams="pkg=74723117-acd4-3e27-8183-2152609aaed7;ver=bbb5224e-151a-11e3-bfef-1b50a66cba06;pos=2">Keeping the Peace: When You &amp; a Co-Worker Want the Same Promotion</a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/the-daily-muse-ycn-1561272/" mapleultparams="pos=2">The Daily Muse</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/secrets-to-your-success/">Secrets to Your Success</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2013-09-03T17:53:00Z">Tue, Sep 3, 2013 1:53 PM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/secrets-to-your-success/keeping-peace-38-co-worker-want-same-promotion-175300121.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>
             </div>
             <div class="bd">
              <p></p>
              <div class="yom-figure yom-fig-left" style="width:310px;">
               <img src="http://l1.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/c8DYE7Md0_RZLXytcLY_2g--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTMxMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/blogs/partner/470_2683293.jpg" id="2683293" name="2683293" title="Want the Same Promotion " height="310" width="310" />
               <p class="legend">Want the Same Promotion </p>
              </div>
              <p></p>
              <p> Opportunities for promotion don't come around very often, so when they do, you may find yourself competing with a colleague for the same spot. Suddenly, your congenial workplace can turn into an episode of <span>Survivor: The Concrete Jungle, with each person gunning for his or her own success at the expense of everything and everyone else.</span></p>
              <p> Fortunately, though, you don't have to choose between getting a raise and maintaining a good relationship. We've outlined three of the common mistakes people make in this scenario that can quickly turn office friends into office frenemies. <br /></p>
              <h3> Mistake #1: Saying Nothing</h3>
              <p> While this strategy might (emphasis on might) minimize conflict, it can also put a lot of strain on your relationship. After all, it's hard to maintain good rapport when you're tip-toeing around such a major issue or fearing that another co-worker <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.thedailymuse.com/career/walk-of-shame-how-to-handle-the-morning-after-happy-hour/">will bring the topic up at happy hour</a>. <br /><br /></p>
              <h5> <em>Our Solution</em></h5>
              <p> Don't let the awkwardness build. A simple, &quot;Hey, I heard that you're applying for that <span>Projec</span></p>...
              <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/keeping-peace-38-co-worker-want-same-promotion-175300121.html" class="read-more" mapleultparams="pkg=74723117-acd4-3e27-8183-2152609aaed7;ver=bbb5224e-151a-11e3-bfef-1b50a66cba06;pos=2">Read More&nbsp;&raquo;</a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <hr /></li>
           <li class="newpage yom-featuredroll-content yom-featuredroll-MediaModelStory">
            <div class="yom-mod" id="mediafeaturedrolllpcatemp">
             <div class="hd">
              <div class="yom-featuredroll-hd">
               <div class="headline">
                <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/actress-nancy-allen-finds-passion-cancer-advocate-040200651.html" mapleultparams="pkg=713e850f-e922-34e4-822d-f26e5bfe0238;ver=4bbcf875-151c-11e3-85e2-6d1ee7f1560f;pos=3">Actress Nancy Allen Finds New Passion as Cancer Advocate</a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/secrets-to-your-success-ycn-1675353/" mapleultparams="pos=3">Secrets To Your Success</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/secrets-to-your-success/">Secrets to Your Success</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2013-09-04T04:02:00Z">Wed, Sep 4, 2013 12:02 AM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/secrets-to-your-success/actress-nancy-allen-finds-passion-cancer-advocate-040200651.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>
             </div>
             <div class="bd">
              <iframe src="http://shine.yahoo.com/video/playlist/secrets-to-your-success/nancy-allen-hollywood-actress-finding-173000078.html?format=embed&amp;show_carousel=true&amp;player_autoplay=false" data-yom-embed-source="{media_id_1:10d2d0a3-f4ee-3b65-a28c-5ccf000a7c78}" frameborder="0" height="495" width="634"></iframe>
              <p>Nancy Allen began her acting career in commercials and went on to score roles in big films including &quot;Carrie,&quot; &quot;Blow Out,&quot; and &quot;Robocop. She was even nominated for a Golden Globe for her role in the movie, &quot;Dressed to Kill.&quot; But a request from a good friend--and cancer survivor--changed her path in life.<br /><br />&quot;If someone had said to me, you know, at some point in your life you're going to be a program director and then an executive director at a cancer support center, I would have said it's never happening ... I know nothing about that,&quot; said Allen. &quot;But everything in my life led me to being right here today. &quot;<br /><br /><a rel="nofollow" href="http://shine.yahoo.com/secrets-to-your-success/wounded-warrior-turns-life-changing-injury-inspiration-035100572.html">More on Shine: Wounded Warrior Turns Life-Changing Injury into Inspiration</a><br /><br />Allen's friend, Wendie, is a cancer survivor, and asked for her help in starting a cancer support center. &quot;It was a time in my life where, I think, I was getting not tired of acting, but tired of the business of it all. And I needed something that had a little more purpose. We would meet here everyday and make ph</p>...
              <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/actress-nancy-allen-finds-passion-cancer-advocate-040200651.html" class="read-more" mapleultparams="pkg=713e850f-e922-34e4-822d-f26e5bfe0238;ver=4bbcf875-151c-11e3-85e2-6d1ee7f1560f;pos=3">Read More&nbsp;&raquo;</a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <hr /></li>
           <li class="newpage yom-featuredroll-content yom-featuredroll-MediaModelStory">
            <div class="yom-mod" id="mediafeaturedrolllpcatemp">
             <div class="hd">
              <div class="yom-featuredroll-hd">
               <div class="headline">
                <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/using-standing-desk-revolutionize-life-184600657.html" mapleultparams="pkg=5e50bbe9-0b15-3c5c-bcc4-455c792f6646;ver=5eb16167-10f2-11e3-bfdd-b876480bf01b;pos=4">Is Standing Up the Best Move You Can Make at Work?</a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/sarah-b-weir-shine-senior-writer-ycn-1203705/" mapleultparams="pos=4">Sarah B. Weir, Shine Senior Writer</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/secrets-to-your-success/">Secrets to Your Success</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2013-08-29T18:46:00Z">Thu, Aug 29, 2013 2:46 PM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/secrets-to-your-success/using-standing-desk-revolutionize-life-184600657.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>
             </div>
             <div class="bd">
              <span id="yui_3_0_0-2-1377802670244222" class="yui-editorial-embed"><span id="yui_3_0_0-2-1377802534971227" class="yui-editorial-embed">
                <div class="yom-fig-frame" style="width:100%;text-align:center;margin:auto;">
                 <div class="yom-figure yom-fig-middle" style="width:630px;">
                  <img title="Are we at a standing desk tipping point? (Getty Image)" alt="" class="editorial " src="http://l.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/lQHgT5ONojE3ko4na_WdtA--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTYzMA--/http://l.yimg.com/os/publish-images/lifestyles/2013-08-29/059f10de-d4ea-4cb8-830e-a12dfe681f2f_standing-desk.jpg" width="630" />
                  <p class="legend">Are we at a standing desk tipping point? (Getty Image)</p>
                 </div>
                </div></span>Anyone who works in a large office has probably noticed colleagues' heads popping up over cubicle dividers like mushrooms sprouting as more and more employees are switching to standing desks (</span>
              <span id="yui_3_0_0-2-1377802670244222" class="yui-editorial-embed"><span id="yui_3_0_0-2-1377802670244222" class="yui-editorial-embed">or jerry-rigging their current regular desks into standing versions)</span>. The trend started a few years ago with mainly geeky tech types touting the benefits of standing at work, and offering their <a rel="nofollow" href="http://lifehacker.com/tag/standing-desk">DIY desk hacks online</a>. Standing desks soon became more mainstream after a <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2012/04/29/sunday-review/stand-up-for-fitness.html?_r=0">number of studies</a> showed </span>
              <span id="yui_3_0_0-2-1377802670244222" class="yui-editorial-embed">the dire health consequences of being a couch—or an office chair—potato. Sure, we've all heard that our modern, sedentary lifestyle has been linked to heart disease, diabetes, and cancer, but one of the most surprising bits of research showed that regular vigorous exercise, long assumed to be a cure for the common office job, <a rel="nofollow" href="http://health.usnews.com/health-news/news/articles/2012/10/15/sitting-can-harm-health-even-for-those-who-exercise">barely mitigated the health risks</a> of sitting for long periods.<p> More on Yahoo: <a rel="nofollow" href="http://yhoo.it/142S6ep">Our Titanic Obesity Problem</a></p><p> This week, diet and exercise app developer <a rel="nofollow" href="http://arshadchowdhury.com/1485-what-happens-when-you-stand-for-2-years/">Arshad Chowdhury, 37, posted a blog</a> th</p></span>...
              <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/using-standing-desk-revolutionize-life-184600657.html" class="read-more" mapleultparams="pkg=5e50bbe9-0b15-3c5c-bcc4-455c792f6646;ver=5eb16167-10f2-11e3-bfdd-b876480bf01b;pos=4">Read More&nbsp;&raquo;</a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <hr /></li>
           <li class="newpage yom-featuredroll-content yom-featuredroll-MediaModelStory">
            <div class="yom-mod" id="mediafeaturedrolllpcatemp">
             <div class="hd">
              <div class="yom-featuredroll-hd">
               <div class="headline">
                <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/bad-manager-3-ways-control-202300486.html" mapleultparams="pkg=d40eb567-be71-3bfa-91bf-8aec1eee06ac;ver=a6b3566b-10db-11e3-b8e6-23bded9479a9;pos=5">Bad Manager? 3 Ways to Take Control</a>
               </div>
              </div>
              <cite class="byline vcard">By <span class="fn"><a href="/blogs/author/the-daily-muse-ycn-1561272/" mapleultparams="pos=5">The Daily Muse</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<span class="provider org"><a href="/blogs/secrets-to-your-success/">Secrets to Your Success</a></span>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<abbr title="2013-08-23T20:23:00Z">Fri, Aug 23, 2013 4:23 PM EDT</abbr>&nbsp;|&nbsp;<a class="comment-count" href="/secrets-to-your-success/bad-manager-3-ways-control-202300486.html#comments">Comments</a></cite>
             </div>
             <div class="bd">
              <p></p>
              <div class="yom-figure yom-fig-left" style="width:310px;">
               <img src="http://l2.yimg.com/bt/api/res/1.2/8BxjxGcmlAlJHhcCOV.jtQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW5ld3M7cT04NTt3PTMxMA--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/blogs/partner/470_2678731.jpg" id="2678731" name="2678731" title="Deal with Bad Manager" height="310" width="310" />
               <p class="legend">Deal with Bad Manager</p>
              </div>
              <p></p>
              <p> If you're feeling unhappy in your 9-to-5, you're not alone. According to <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.gallup.com/strategicconsulting/163007/state-american-workplace.aspx)">t</a><a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.gallup.com/strategicconsulting/163007/state-american-workplace.aspx)">he latest Gallup poll</a>, only three in 10 employees are fully engaged at work. And it's not because of long hours, dull assignments, or a lack of team culture. The biggest culprit? Terrible managers.</p>
              <p> A whopping 75% of employees say their manager is their <a rel="nofollow" href="http://usatoday30.usatoday.com/news/health/story/2012-08-05/apa-mean-bosses/56813062/1practice%20of%20putting%20the%20wrong%20managers%20in%20place">biggest source of stress at work</a>, and 65% of employees <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/story/two-thirds-america-unhappy-at-job-65-choose-new-boss-over-raise-says-study-by-tellyourbosscom-2012-10-16">would rather have a new manager</a> than a raise.</p>
              <p> Sound shocking? Not when you look at it from the other side-turns out, managers are also struggling. Only one in 10 leaders is actually <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.hcareers.com/us/resourcecenter/tabid/306/articleid/876/default.aspx">groomed for the job</a>-but then again, half took the role solely to snag a raise; only 23% actually wanted to lead a team.</p>
              <p> Yikes.</p>
              <p> So, if you're stuck with a <span>less-than-ideal boss</span>, what can you do? Well, you can either let this manager mayhem make your life a miserable daymare (like a nightmare, only with sunshine), or you can accept that the game has changed and adjust your action plan accordingly. I would strongly suggest the latter-s</p>...
              <a href="/secrets-to-your-success/bad-manager-3-ways-control-202300486.html" class="read-more" mapleultparams="pkg=d40eb567-be71-3bfa-91bf-8aec1eee06ac;ver=a6b3566b-10db-11e3-b8e6-23bded9479a9;pos=5">Read More&nbsp;&raquo;</a>
             </div>
            </div>
            <hr /></li>
          </ul>
         </div>

    <div class="text"> 
     <h3>Dr. Temple Grandin to Visit UC Riverside</h3> 
     <div class="text-body"> 
      <p><img src="http://media.tumblr.com/1c267e0941ab1755a571aaf0738068a8/tumblr_inline_mm30iiNeFG1qz4rgp.jpg" /></p> 
      <p class="MsoNormal"><span>The country’s leading animal behaviorist and autism expert, <strong>Dr. Temple Grandin </strong></span>will speak at the University of California, Riverside on <strong>Tuesday, May 21, at 7 p.m. </strong>in Highlander Union Building, Room 302. She will be introduced by Dr. Jan Blacher, Distinguished Professor and Director of SEARCH, the University of California’s first family autism resource center housed in the Graduate School of Education. <span>&nbsp;</span></p> 
      <p><span>This event is free and open to the public. <span>&nbsp;</span>No tickets will be issued so arriving early is strongly recommended. Doors will open at 6pm. Parking for non-UC permit holders costs $5 in Lot 1.<span>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p> 
      <p></p> 
      <p class="read_more_container"><a href="http://ucriversidepresents.tumblr.com/post/49272726747/dr-temple-grandin-to-visit-uc-riverside" class="read_more">Read More</a></p> 
     </div> 
    </div>

    </div> 
    <!-- end .date --> 
    <div class="text"> 
     <h3>David Wax Museum - March 7, 8pm </h3> 
     <div class="text-body"> 
      <p class="MsoNormal"><span>David Wax Museum’s sound tests the boundaries of easy categorization. Singer and guitarist <strong>David Wax</strong> and bandmate <strong>Suz Slezak</strong> (vocals and violin) have cultivated a Mexo-American aesthetic by fusing their knowledge of Mexican folk music with American roots and indie rock. The two crafted their unique sound in and around Boston clubs and in rural Veracruz, Mexico when Wax received a graduate fellowship to study regional musical styles including <em>son jarocho</em>. Slezak, who sings lead, also takes turns playing a fiddle and a traditional Mexican instrument called a <em>guijada</em>, which is fashioned from the jawbone of a donkey. The result is an irrepressible combination of harmonies, Mexican rhythms, and rootsy sound that has become an artistic triumph, earning the winsome duo a spot at the </span><span>prestigious Newport Folk Festival and the 2010 Boston Music Award for Best Americana Artist. Learn more: www.</span><span> <a href="http://www.davidwaxmuseum.com/"></a><a href="http://www.davidwaxmuseum.com/">http://www.davidwaxmuseum.com/</a></span><span></span></p> 
      <p><img alt="David Wax Museum" height="1500" src="http://www.davidwaxmuseum.com/wordpress/wp-content/gallery/shorefire/dwm_tr-34_20120618_151757.jpg" width="1000" /><span>March 7, 2013, 8&nbsp;pm<br /><a href="http://www.culvercenter.ucr.edu/" title="Culver Center of the Arts">Culver Center of the Arts</a><br /> Free </span></p> 
      <p><span><a href="http://maps.google.com/maps?hl=en&amp;gl=us&amp;daddr=3834+Main+Street,+Riverside,+CA+92501&amp;panel=1&amp;f=d&amp;fb=1&amp;dirflg=d&amp;geocode=0,33.981264,-117.374450&amp;cid=0,0,875492350631520353&amp;hq=culver+center+of+the+arts&amp;hnear=0x80dca6df7ff47dbb:0xf7a1d705135e0ae8,Riverside,+CA&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=6FB0UPr_NsjRiAL_xoCICA&amp;ved=0CHUQngIwAA%20" title="map view">map</a></span></p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <!-- end .text --> 
    <ul class="post-footer">

    <!-- end .date --> 
    <div class="text"> 
     <h3>VICTOIRE in concert JAN 23, 2013 [ free! ] </h3> 
     <div class="text-body"> 
      <p><strong><span><a href="http://www.victoiremusic.com/">VICTOIRE</a></span></strong><span>, a Brooklyn-based band founded by composer Missy Mazzoli, has been dubbed an “all-star, all-female quintet” by Time Out New York. This quirky ensemble combines strings, clarinets, keyboards and lo-fi electronics (including samples of sewing machines and answering machine tapes) to create their “minimalist, post-rock bliss”. Victoire is as much a child of composer <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Philip+Glass">Philip Glass</a> as of instrumental post-rock ensembles <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Godspeed+You!+Black+Emperor">Godspeed You! Black Emperor</a>, and <a href="http://www.last.fm/music/Sigur+R%C3%B3s">Sigur R&oacute;s</a>. They’ve been making waves in New York’s downtown music scene for several years. Members of Victoire have performed at BAM, Carnegie Hall, Lincoln Center, and other prestigious venues around the world. Their debut album, Cathedral City, released on New Amsterdam Records was the hit-darling of 2010, making several top-ten lists including NPR’s best classical album and The New Yorker’s most memorable album lists. <span>&nbsp;</span></span></p> 
      <p><span>Unique to Victoire’s west-coast concert at the Culver Center is an exciting collaboration with UCR MFA dance students</span><span>&nbsp;</span><span>who will </span><span>channel the free-spirited ensemble’s waves of sound in live performance. Their conceptualized choreography will provide a seamless conversation of movement matching the tone, structure, and imagery of Victoire’s immersive and imaginative soundscape.</span></p> 
      <p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span>Wednesday, January 23, 2013</span></strong><span>, <strong>8 PM - <u>FREE</u></strong> <br /></span><span><a href="http://www.culvercenter.ucr.edu/" title="Culver Center"><span>Culver Center of the Arts</span></a><br /></span><span>3834 Main Street, Riverside, CA 92501</span></p> 
      <p class="MsoNoSpacing"><em><span>Seating is first come, first served</span></em><span>.</span></p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <!-- end .text -->

     <h3>Josh Kornbluth, comic monologuist and filmmaker - April 21</h3> 
     <div class="text-body"> 
      <p><strong><img src="http://media.tumblr.com/tumblr_mbmxoeNfqJ1rxdq17.jpg" /></strong></p> 
      <p><strong><a href="http://www.joshkornbluth.com/" title="Josh Kornbluth">JOSH KORNBLUTH</a>: THE MATHEMATICS OF CHANGE</strong></p> 
      <p>A comic monologue that recounts the uproarious experiences of a Princeton University would-be math whiz who discovers his limits in freshman calculus.&nbsp;</p> 
      <p>April 21, 2013, 4pm<br /><span><a href="http://www.culvercenter.ucr.edu" title="Culver Center of the Arts">Culver Center of the Arts</a>&nbsp;- 3834 Main Street, Riverside <br /></span><span>Free <span>&nbsp;</span><span>&nbsp;</span></span></p> 
      <p><a href="http://maps.google.com/maps?hl=en&amp;gl=us&amp;daddr=3834+Main+Street,+Riverside,+CA+92501&amp;panel=1&amp;f=d&amp;fb=1&amp;dirflg=d&amp;geocode=0,33.981264,-117.374450&amp;cid=0,0,875492350631520353&amp;hq=culver+center+of+the+arts&amp;hnear=0x80dca6df7ff47dbb:0xf7a1d705135e0ae8,Riverside,+CA&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=6FB0UPr_NsjRiAL_xoCICA&amp;ved=0CHUQngIwAA%20" title="map view">map</a></p>

     <h3>The Calder Quartet - February 17</h3> 
     <div class="text-body"> 
      <p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span><img src="http://media.tumblr.com/tumblr_mbmy7xQIxi1rxdq17.jpg" />&nbsp;</span></strong></p> 
      <p class="MsoNormal"><a href="http://calderquartet.com/">BENJAMIN JACOBSON</a>, violin <br /><a href="http://calderquartet.com/">ANDREW BULBROOK</a>, violin <br /><a href="http://calderquartet.com/">JONATHAN MOERSCHEL</a>, viola <br /><a href="http://calderquartet.com/">ERIC BYERS</a>, cello</p> 
      <p class="MsoNormal">Like the iconic mobiles, this superb quartet relies on the motion of interrelated shapes to balance one piece of music against another so that each reveals something new.</p> 
      <p>February 17, 2013,&nbsp;4&nbsp;pm<br /><span><a href="http://www.culvercenter.ucr.edu" title="Culver Center of the Arts">Culver Center of the Arts</a><br /></span><span>Free&nbsp;<span>&nbsp;</span><span>&nbsp;</span></span></p> 
      <p><span><span><a href="http://maps.google.com/maps?hl=en&amp;gl=us&amp;daddr=3834+Main+Street,+Riverside,+CA+92501&amp;panel=1&amp;f=d&amp;fb=1&amp;dirflg=d&amp;geocode=0,33.981264,-117.374450&amp;cid=0,0,875492350631520353&amp;hq=culver+center+of+the+arts&amp;hnear=0x80dca6df7ff47dbb:0xf7a1d705135e0ae8,Riverside,+CA&amp;sa=X&amp;ei=6FB0UPr_NsjRiAL_xoCICA&amp;ved=0CHUQngIwAA%20" title="map view">map</a></span></span></p>

   <div class="post"> 
    <div class="text"> 
     <h3>NPR’s ARI SHAPIRO: The Inside Scoop on the 2012 Election - November 12&nbsp;</h3> 
     <div class="text-body"> 
      <p><img src="http://media.tumblr.com/tumblr_mbmv0tBB3X1rxdq17.jpg" /></p> 
      <p>National Public Radio’s White House Correspondent<br />Award-winning journalist</p> 
      <p><span>For the last several months NPR White House Correspondent <strong>Ari Shapiro</strong> has been traveling with the Romney Campaign and reporting on the candidate’s every move in his quest for the White House. After months inside the press pool covering the resolutely coiffed candidate through the ups and downs of primaries, caucuses, and the general election, Shapiro will offer an insider’s account of everything Election 2012. Learn about the events, people, and experiences that defined the road to the Presidency for a nation of listeners. </span></p> 
      <p class="MsoNormal"><span> November 12, 2012,&nbsp;7&nbsp;pm<br /><span><span><a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=HUB" title="Highlander Union Building">Highlander Union Building, 302</a><br /></span></span></span><span>Free | Parking $5 in Lot 1&nbsp;</span></p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <!-- end .text --> 
    <ul class="post-footer"> 
     <li><a href="http://ucriversidepresents.tumblr.com/post/33234823306/nprs-ari-shapiro-the-inside-scoop-on-the-2012">Permalink</a></li>
